#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress						: Master Progress Variable to track number of months good has spent outside the acceptable price range
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_characters		: Variable tracking characters
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_igs			: Variable tracking interest groups
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_buildings		: Variable tracking buildings
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_legitimacy		: Variable tracking current government legitimacy. Strong government = fast progress variable reduction. Weak government legitimacy = slow or no progress variable reduction
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_effects		: Variable tracking effects from events, etc, that influence the progress Variable
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_price			: Variable tracking market price of good
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_next				: Variable is an incrementor - it is calculated from previous 6 variables (characters, IGs, buildings, government legitimacy, events) on a weekly basis, and is added to uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress on the monthly. Used in localization to tell the player the current rate of change for uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress is.

gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_core_variables = {
	# Used solely for mathematical purposes, and is set as equivalent to the clout
	# of a given interest group. It exists so that IGs can be weighted higher or lower
	# depending on whether they're in government or not
	set_variable = { name = uk_ig_weight value = 0 }

# Aluminum rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_aluminum_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 7 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price }
}

	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game

# Engines rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_engines_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 7 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_igs }

# Iron rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_iron_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 7 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation

# Oil rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_oil_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 7 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price }
}

# Sugar rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_sugar_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_igs value = 0 }

	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good

		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 12 }

	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price }
}

# Wine rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_wine_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 7 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price }
}

gbr_start_rationing_aluminum = {
	# Check that the UK is rationing & not already rationing aluminum
	# Determine whether aluminum needs to be rationed
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_started_rationing
			NOT = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } } }
			NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum }
		}
		set_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
		gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_start_rationing_bauxite = {
	# Check that the UK is rationing & not already rationing bauxite
	# Determine whether bauxite needs to be rationed
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_started_rationing
			NOT = { market_capital.market = { mg:bauxite = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } } }
			NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite }
		}
		set_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite
		gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_start_rationing_fertilizer = {
	# Check that the UK is rationing & not already rationing fertilizer (chemicals)
	# Determine whether fertilizer (chemicals) needs to be rationed
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_started_rationing

		}
		set_variable = uk_rationing_fertilizer
		gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_fertilizer_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_end_rationing_aluminum = {
	# Check to see if rationing for aluminum can be ended
	# aluminum has to be 20% cheaper than base price for 6 months in a row
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } }
			var:uk_ending_aluminum_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_aluminum_rationing add = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } }
			var:uk_ending_aluminum_rationing = var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = united_kingdom_post_war_events.110
			days = 1
		}
		set_variable = uk_aluminum_rationing_finished
		remove_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
		gbr_remove_uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_end_rationing_engines = {
	# Check to see if rationing for engines can be ended
	# engines has to be 20% cheaper than base price for 6 months in a row
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_rationing_engines
			market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } }
			var:uk_ending_engines_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_engines_rationing add = 1 }
	}

		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_rationing_sugar
			market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } }
			var:uk_ending_sugar_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_sugar_rationing add = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_rationing_sugar
			market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.15 } }
			var:uk_ending_sugar_rationing = var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = united_kingdom_post_war_events.139
			days = 1
		}
		set_variable = uk_sugar_rationing_finished
		remove_variable = uk_rationing_sugar
		gbr_remove_uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_rationing_over = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
				has_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fertilizer
				has_variable = uk_rationing_clothes
				has_variable = uk_rationing_coal
				has_variable = uk_rationing_coffee
				has_variable = uk_rationing_copper
				has_variable = uk_rationing_engines
				has_variable = uk_rationing_explosives
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fabric
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fish
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fruit
				has_variable = uk_rationing_glass
				has_variable = uk_rationing_grain
				has_variable = uk_rationing_groceries
				has_variable = uk_rationing_high_quality_fabric
				has_variable = uk_rationing_iron
				has_variable = uk_rationing_lead
				has_variable = uk_rationing_liquor
				has_variable = uk_rationing_meat
				has_variable = uk_rationing_oil
				has_variable = uk_rationing_opium
				has_variable = uk_rationing_paper
				has_variable = uk_rationing_pharmaceuticals
				has_variable = uk_rationing_phosphorus
				has_variable = uk_rationing_plastics
				has_variable = uk_rationing_refined_fuel
				has_variable = uk_rationing_rubber
				has_variable = uk_rationing_steel
				has_variable = uk_rationing_sugar
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tea
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tobacco
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tools
				has_variable = uk_rationing_wine
				has_variable = uk_rationing_wood
			}
		}
		set_variable = uk_post_war_rationing_over
	}
}
